<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a> (3607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stoc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stukkaz</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stokken.html>stokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stokje.html>stokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stick, natural (wood) or artificial</li>
<li>cane
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liep.html>liep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a></b>.</i>

***stokbrood.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stokbrood.html>stokbrood</a> (37715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stok.html>stok</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 1910s in advertisements, in particular in the Dutch East Indies and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delft" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Delft"><a href = vnd.unilang:delft.html>Delft</a></a>, but seemingly entering the common vocabulary only in the 1960s and 1970s.
</p>

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stollen.html>stollen</a></span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:stol.html>Stol</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally eaten around Christmas and (since the 1980s, so not quite traditionally) <a href = vnd.unilang:easter.html>Easter</a>. The recipe generally doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> vary <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the holiday, the different names are purely based on marketing.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">feeststol</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kerststol</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">paasstol</span></li></ul>

***stom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a> (763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stummaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stumm</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">stum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stommer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">stomst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mute</span>, unable to speak, as medical condition or species-determined
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sprakeloos.html>sprakeloos</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">speechless</span>; soundless, silent
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sprakeloos.html>sprakeloos</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stil.html>stil</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomme.html>stomme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:films.html>films</a></i>
<dl><dd><i>silent movies</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>wordless, non-verbal
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">woordeloos</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">non-verbaal</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Spotprenten <a href = vnd.unilang:leveren.html>leveren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stomme.html>stomme</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kritiek.html>kritiek</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:cartoons.html>Cartoons</a> often provide <b>non-verbal</b> criticism.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mentally dulling, soul-killing
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstompen.html>afstompend</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geestdodend.html>geestdodend</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>stupid, dumb
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stompzinnig.html>stompzinnig</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">foolish</span>, senseless, piteous
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>in compounds essentially reinforcing the sense</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The use of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:stom.html>stom</a></i> for ‘stupid’ <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> depreciated by the deaf community, since it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the proper word for ‘mute’ in the sense of people who cannot speak. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, however, no less common usage, analogous to the use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dumb</i> in English.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoma.html>stoma</a> (79282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoma.html>stoma</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoma.html>stoma</a>'s</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">stomata</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoma.html>stomaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:stoma.html>stoma</a>, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of the tiny pores in the epidermis of a leaf or <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> through which gases and water vapor pass.</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:stoma.html>stoma</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a <span class="Latn" lang="en">stupidity</span>, a stupid action</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">stupidity</span>, the quality of being stupid
<ul><li><b>1846</b> March 2, "<a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>Geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ezel.html>ezel</a>" (pseudonym), "Arrondissements-Regtbank <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> Middelburg" (continued), <i>Vlissingsche <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a></i>, No. 29 (1846 March 9), page 2.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> wenschten <a href = vnd.unilang:gaarne.html>gaarne</a> dienaangaande eenig <a href = vnd.unilang:uitsluitsel.html>uitsluitsel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>, want <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stommiteit.html>stommiteit</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrijpen.html>begrijpen</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***stoomcursus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoomcursus.html>stoomcursus</a> (87744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stomen.html>stomen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to steam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cursus.html>cursus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">course</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Perhaps in reference to steam engines or to steaming as a relatively quick method of cooking. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klaarstomen.html>klaarstomen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoomcursus.html>stoomcursus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoomcursus.html>stoomcursussen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A very short intensive educational course to prepare students for an exam or a subsequent course or education. <span class="defdate">[from early 20th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A short military course to prepare regular <a href = vnd.unilang:soldiers.html>soldiers</a> or recruits for an officer education. <span class="defdate">[from late 19th c.]</span></li></ol>

***stoot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoot.html>stoot</a> (4308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stôot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*stauti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stautiz</i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoten.html>stoten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoot.html>stoot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoten.html>stoten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoot.html>stootje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a jab, punch, blow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">billiards</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a shot</li>
<li>a stab with a pointed object</li>
<li>a shocking interruption of a movement, shock</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thrust (single penetrating movement of the <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a> during sex.)</li></ol>

***stop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> (350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoppen.html>stoppe</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoppen.html>stoppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An action of stopping, cessation.</li>
<li>A plug for a sink, a <a href = vnd.unilang:stopper.html>stopper</a>.</li>
<li>An electric fuse.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zekering.html>zekering</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoplicht.html>stoplicht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoplichten.html>stoplichten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoplicht.html>stoplichtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">traffic light</span>.</li>
<li>One of the lights on a traffic light or on another signalling device, in particular a red one.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoppen.html>stoppen</a> (487)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoppen.html>stoppen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stuppon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stuppōną</i>. ***storen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:storen.html>storen</a> (2601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stôren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stōren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*staurijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***storm.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a> (2043)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sturmaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stormen.html>stormen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stormpje.html>stormpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:storm.html>storm</a></a>; a wind scale for very strong wind, stronger than a gale, less than a hurricane.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of sieges or battles</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> assault, storming
